FNV NATIVE DIRECTIONAL LIGHT ALIAS AUDIT

Source claims being tested:
- Reloaded NewVegas Game.h: Sun +0x1C is the same pointer as Main/TES +0x1C directionalLight.
- Reloaded GameNi.h: NiLight +0xD4 is diffuse color and NiDirectionalLight +0xF0 is direction.

Questions:
1. Which methods are in the Sun vtable rooted at 0x0104F298?
2. Does native executable code copy or compare Sun +0x1C and Main/TES +0x1C?
3. Are Main/TES +0x1C reads/writes specific to directional light, or only generic cleanup?
4. Does any proven aliased object read stable +0xD4 diffuse color or +0xF0 direction fields?

Do not promote NVR header fields into Psycho constants unless this output proves the native alias.
